msg:What this store does better is the service and the environment. But the sanitation is average, there are uncleaned cigarette butts in the obvious places of the room, and the bathroom smell is serious. The room facilities are complete, but they are quite old, and the TV cannot be projected on the screen, let alone intelligent facilities. Such a large hotel does not even have a service robot. The linen is clean, but the toiletries are lakwa. It may be the best hotel in Changyi, but the price/performance ratio is really low.
